***cranium.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>cranium</a> (94403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crānium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρανίον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kraníon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>cranium</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">craniums</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">crania</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The braincase or neurocranium; that part of the skull consisting of the <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a> enclosing the brain, but not including the <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a> of the face or jaw.
<ul><li><b>1858</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Gray, <i>Anatomy: Descriptive and Surgical</i>, "The Skull", page 19.
<dl><dd>The Skull <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> divided into two parts, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>Cranium</a></b> and the Face. The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>Cranium</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> composed of <i>eight</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a>; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1908</b>, J. McFadyean, <i>The Comparative Anatomy of the Domesticated Animals</i>, Part I: Osteology and Arthrology, "Skeleton of Fowl", page 165.
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>cranium</a></b> of the fowl <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> composed of the same elements as are present in the mammalian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>cranium</a></b>, save that there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no interparietal.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:elaine.html>Elaine</a> N. Marieb amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:katja.html>Katja</a> Hoehn, <i>Human Anatomy and Physiology</i>, 8th ed., Chapter 7 "The Skeleton", page 200
<dl><dd>The cranial <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a>, or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>cranium</a></b> (kra′ne-um), enclose and protect the fragile brain and furnish attachment sites for head and neck muscles.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anthropology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The upper portion of the skull, including the neurocranium and facial <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a>, but not including the jawbone (mandible).
<ul><li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:emma.html>Emma</a> L. Brown, Ronald A. Dixon, amp; Jason W. Birkett, "The Discolouration of Human Teeth from Archaeological Contexts: Elemental Analysis of a Black Tooth from a Roman <a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>Cranium</a> Recovered from the River Witham, Lincoln, UK", <i>Journal of Anthropology</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 2014, Article ID 859153, 7 pages. <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://doi.org/10.1155/2014/859153">https://doi.org/10.1155/2014/859153</a>.
<dl><dd>In this study, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cranium.html>cranium</a></b> recovered from the River Witham in Lincoln exhibited a black metallic staining on the surfaces of the teeth.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The skull.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">braincase</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">neurocranium</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">skull</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">skull</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:credo.html>credo</a> (25864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crede</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:credo.html>credo</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crēdō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:credo.html>credo</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:credo.html>credo</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:credo.html>credootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">confession</span> of  <span class="Latn" lang="en">faith</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">creed</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belijdenis.html>belijdenis</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloofsbelijdenis.html>geloofsbelijdenis</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (strong) <span class="Latn" lang="en">conviction</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overtuiging.html>overtuiging</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crematorium.html>crematorium</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crematorium.html>crematoria</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">crematoriums</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crematorium.html>crematoriumpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***crimineel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:crimineel.html>crimineel</a> (3078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crimineel.html>crimineel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crimineler.html>crimineler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">crimineelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>criminal, contrary to enforceable legal rules</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> terrible, excessive (generally in a bad sense)</li></ol>

***criterium.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:criterium.html>criterium</a> (43941)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">critērium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κριτήριον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kritḗrion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:criterium.html>criterium</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:criteria.html>criteria</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:criteriums.html>criteriums</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:criterium.html>criteriumpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(plural <a href = vnd.unilang:criteria.html>criteria</a>) criterion, standard for comparison and appreciation</li>
<li>(plural <a href = vnd.unilang:criteriums.html>criteriums</a>) notably in cycling, race of low athletic merit</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">criterion</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">falsifieerbaarheidscriterium</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:croissant.html>croissant</a> (33476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:croissant.html>croissant</a></i>, present participle of verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">croître</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:croissant.html>croissant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:croissants.html>croissants</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:croissant.html>croissantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***crossbow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:crossbow.html>crossbow</a> (43940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">crosbowe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">crossebowe</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cross</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:crossbow.html>crossbow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">crossbows</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mechanised weapon, based on the bow and arrow, that shoots bolts.</li>
<li>A portable ballista that can be <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> in the hand.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">crossbowman</span></li></ul>

***crossroads.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a> (65546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">crossroad</i></span></span></li>
<li>A place where one road crosses another; an intersection of two or more roads.
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, M. K. Hobson, <i>The Native Star</i>:
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">When they <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></b> where the road split off into four cardinal directions, Stanton stood squinting up at the signpost for a long time.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A centrally located position
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jake.html>Jake</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:logan.html>Logan</a>, <i>Slocum and the Sierra <a href = vnd.unilang:madras.html>Madras</a> Gold</i>:
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The shiny <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> black triangle at the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></b> of where her <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> split.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2018</b>, Rail, issue 857, July 18-July 31, article on Severn Bridge Junction signal box at Shrewsbury:
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Together they control the approaches to this important railway <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></b> from Chester, <a href = vnd.unilang:crewe.html>Crewe</a>, Wolverhampton, <a href = vnd.unilang:hereford.html>Hereford</a> and Machynlleth, and the station itself <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> an unusual mix of semaphore and colour light signals.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by analogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A decision point; a turning point or opportunity to change direction, course, or goal.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nonstandard</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fork in the road.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1955</b>,  Therese Pol,  <cite>The judge and his hangman</cite>, translation of original by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Friedrich_D%C3%BCrrenmatt" class="extiw" title="w:Friedrich Dürrenmatt">Friedrich Dürrenmatt</a>, page 48:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But first he stopped his car at the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></b> where the highway forked off to Gastmann's house.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:phil.html>Phil</a> Nordyke,  <cite>All American, all the way: the combat history of the 82nd Airborne</cite>, page 723:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Company A commander, <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a> Helmer, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> at the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></b> where the road split, with the left fork leading to Udenbreth, when he saw a group of <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> coming toward him.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  Raeanne Thayne,  <cite>A Cold Creek <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>Baby</a></cite>, page 199:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">When she reached the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crossroads.html>crossroads</a></b> where the trail split, one part of her yearned to head toward the lake.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:croupier.html>croupier</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/croupier" class="extiw" title="w:croupier"><a href = vnd.unilang:croupier.html>croupier</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/croupier" class="extiw" title="w:croupier">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:croupier.html>croupier</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:croupiers.html>croupiers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The person who collects bets and pays out winnings at a gambling table, such as in a <a href = vnd.unilang:casino.html>casino</a>.</li>
<li>One who, at a public dinner party, sits at the lower end of the table as assistant chairman.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a> (76582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crypta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vault</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρυπτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kruptós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hidden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grotto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">crypts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cave or cavern. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span></li>
<li>An underground vault, especially one beneath a church that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a burial place. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Arlen" class="extiw" title="w:Michael Arlen">Michael Arlen</a>,  “3/2/1”, in  <cite>“Piracy”: A Romantic Chronicle of These Days</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1519647W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> and waved a hand to him, she cried a word, but he didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> hear it, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> word. A sable <a href = vnd.unilang:wraith.html>wraith</a> she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in the parkland, fading away into the dolorous <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a> </b> of winter.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Andrew Martin,  <cite>Underground Overground: A passenger's history of the Tube</cite>, Profile Books, →ISBN, page 106:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">On its arrival at Bank, incidentally, the City amp; South London's directors <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> threatened to demolish the church of St <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Woolnoth, but after a public outcry the company built its station in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a></b> of the church, the <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> being transferred [...]. Therefore St <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Woolnoth doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a></b>. Or you could say that its <b><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Bank station.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small pit or cavity in the surface of an organ or other structure. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>2015</b>, David Shaw, translating Giulia <a href = vnd.unilang:enders.html>Enders</a>, <i>Gut</i>, Scribe 2016, p. 25:
<dl><dd>Sometimes, too much foreign material can get caught in the <b>crypts</b>, leading to frequent infections.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a> of Lieberkühn</span></li>
<li>hemicrypt</li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:crypt.html>crypt</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergrondse.html>ondergrondse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruimte.html>ruimte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koor.html>koor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerk.html>kerk</a></li></ol>

***crypte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:crypte.html>crypte</a> (19036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crypta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρυπτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kruptós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">krocht</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grot.html>grot</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gruft</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypte.html>crypte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypte.html>cryptes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypte.html>cryptetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***cuckoo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> (76578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cokkou</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cucu</i> (whence French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">coucou</i>); ultimately onomatopoeic, perhaps <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cucūlus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cuckoos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>, of the family Cuculidae, famous for laying its eggs in the nests of other species; but especially the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/common_cuckoo" class="extiw" title="w:common cuckoo">common <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></a>, <i>Cuculus canorus</i>, that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a characteristic two-note call.
<ul><li><b>1596-97</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Merchant_of_Venice" class="extiw" title="w:The Merchant of Venice">The Merchant of Venice</a></i>, Act V Scene 1
<dl><dd>He knows <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, as the <a href = vnd.unilang:blind.html>blind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> knows the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></b>, / By the bad voice.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The sound of that particular bird.</li>
<li>The bird-shaped figure found in <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> clocks.</li>
<li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> clock itself.</li>
<li>A person who inveigles themselves into a place where they should not be (used especially in the phrase <i>a <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> in the nest</i>).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> crazy.</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">coo-coo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Barbadian food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> clock</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cuckoo-dove</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cuckoo-pint</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><i>Arum italicum</i></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cuckoo_shrike" class="extiw" title="w:cuckoo shrike"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a></a></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a>'s egg</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cloud-cuckoo-land</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cuculine</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a> sign</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">cuckoos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cuckooing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cuckooed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make the call of a <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a>.</li>
<li>To repeat something incessantly. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> add an example for this sense?)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:cuckoo.html>cuckoo</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Crazy; not sane.</li></ol>

***cultus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cultus.html>cultus</a> (22881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultus.html>cultus</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultus.html>cultus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultussen.html>cultussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultus.html>cultusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cult</span>, a particular tradition of worship or veneration of deities, ancestors, <a href = vnd.unilang:guardians.html>guardians</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:saints.html>saints</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> religious service</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>For the pejorative sense of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cult</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">socially marginal, proscribed or deviant religious group</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sekte.html>sekte</a></i>.</li></ul>

***cultuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuur</a> (4262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">culture</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cultivation; culture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cultūra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cultivation; culture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultus.html>cultus</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">colō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">till, cultivate, worship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">colōnus</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">colōnia</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move; to turn (around)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:culturen.html>culturen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">culture</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">practices and beliefs particular to a society or group</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">culture</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a>, historic heritage and media as a sector</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">culture</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">cultivation</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tillage of crops</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">culture</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">collective of microorganisms</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
